<p>行高缩放基数样式枚举。默认样式为TEXT_LINE_HEIGHT_BY_FONT_SIZE。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 21</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">枚举项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TEXT_LINE_HEIGHT_BY_FONT_SIZE = 0</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>以字号大小作为缩放基数。</p> <p>行高计算公式：FontSize * FontHeight。</p> <p>FontSize可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstylegetfontsize">OH_Drawing_TextStyleGetFontSize</a>接口获取。</p> <p>FontHeight可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstylegetfontheight">OH_Drawing_TextStyleGetFontHeight</a>接口获取。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TEXT_LINE_HEIGHT_BY_FONT_HEIGHT = 1</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>以字形高度作为缩放基数。</p> <p>行高计算公式：字形高度 * FontHeight。</p> <p>字形高度由文本经过字体文件塑形得到。</p> <p>FontHeight（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstylegetfontheight">OH_Drawing_TextStyleGetFontHeight</a>获取）。</p> </td> </tr> class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">枚举项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TEXT_STYLE_ATTR_D_LINE_HEIGHT_MAXIMUM = 0</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>行高上限。</p> <p>若同时开启行高缩放，当FontHeight（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstylegetfontheight">OH_Drawing_TextStyleGetFontHeight</a>接口获取）大于0时行高上限才生效。</p> <p>取值范围为单精度浮点数正数部分，默认值为单精度浮点数上限。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TEXT_STYLE_ATTR_D_LINE_HEIGHT_MINIMUM = 1</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>行高下限。</p> <p>取值范围为单精度浮点数非负部分，默认值为0。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TEXT_STYLE_ATTR_I_LINE_HEIGHT_STYLE = 2</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">行高缩放基数样式。具体行高缩放基数样式可见<a _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="handle-button class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-jay-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-cpp" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">enum</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">OH_Drawing_TypographyStyleAttributeId</span></li></ol></pre></div></div> <p><strong>描述</strong></p> <p>排版样式属性枚举。</p> <p>针对排版样式和文本样式中的共有属性，建议优先使用文本样式属性（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstyleattributeid">OH_Drawing_TextStyleAttributeId</a>获取）。</p> <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 21</p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">枚举项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TYPOGRAPHY_STYLE_ATTR_D_LINE_HEIGHT_MAXIMUM = 0</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>行高上限。</p> <p>若同时开启行高缩放，当FontHeight（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstylegetfontheight">OH_Drawing_TextStyleGetFontHeight</a>接口获取）大于0时行高上限才生效。</p> <p>取值范围为单精度浮点数正数部分。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TYPOGRAPHY_STYLE_ATTR_D_LINE_HEIGHT_MINIMUM = 1</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>行高下限。</p> <p>若同时开启行高缩放，当FontHeight（可由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_textstylegetfontheight">OH_Drawing_TextStyleGetFontHeight</a>接口获取）大于0时行高下限才生效。</p> <p>取值范围为单精度浮点数非负部分，默认值为0。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TYPOGRAPHY_STYLE_ATTR_D_LINE_SPACING = 2</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>行间距。</p> <p>lineSpacing不受行高上下限的限制。</p> <p>尾行默认添加行间距。</p> <p>可通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_typographytextsetheightbehavior">OH_Drawing_TypographyTextSetHeightBehavior</a>接口设置textHeightBehavior为DISABLE_LAST_ASCENT禁用尾行行间距。</p> <p>默认值为0。</p> </td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TYPOGRAPHY_STYLE_ATTR_I_LINE_HEIGHT_STYLE = 3</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">行高缩放基数样式。具体行高缩放基数样式可见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_lineheightstyle">OH_Drawing_LineHeightStyle</a>。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">TYPOGRAPHY_STYLE_ATTR_I_FONT_WIDTH = 4</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">字宽。</td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int fontWeight</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>设置字重，设置0字重为thin，设置1字重为extra-light，设置2字重为light，设置4字重为medium，设置5字重为semi-bold，</p> <p>设置排版样式默认字重。目前只有系统默认字体支持字重的调节，其他字体设置字重值小于semi-bold时字体粗细无变化，当设置字重值大于等于semi-bold时可能会触发伪加粗效果。</p> <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Graphic.Graphic2D.NativeDrawing</p> class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int weight</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>设置字重，设置0字重为thin，设置1字重为extra-light，设置2字重为light，设置4字重为medium，设置5字重为semi-bold，</p> <p>设置6字重为bold，设置7字重为extra-bold，设置8字重为black，设置3或其它字重为normal/regular，具体可见<a <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 12</p> <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>  <div class="tablenoborder"><div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> <tbody><tr class="firstRow"><th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.159.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th> <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.159.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th> </tr><tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-oh-drawing-textstyle">OH_Drawing_TextStyle</a>* style</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指向OH_Drawing_TextStyle对象的指针，由<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_createtextstyle">OH_Drawing_CreateTextStyle</a>获取。</td> </tr> <tr><td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">const <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-oh-drawing-rectstyle-info">OH_Drawing_RectStyle_Info</a>* width="50%">int styleId</td> <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><p>要设置的样式id，仅当背景框为圆角矩形时有效。文本处理时会被划分为多个分段，每个分段都有自己的TextStyle，id标识着这个分段将被绘制于第几个背景矩形框中。</p> <p>若一行中每个分段的id全为0，表示所有分段绘制在同一个圆角矩形背景框中；若一行中的id为0, 1，则id为0的分段绘制在一个圆角矩形背景框内，id为1的分段绘制在另一个圆角矩形背景框内，以此类推。</p> </td> </tr>  </tbody></table></div> </div> </div>  <div class="tiledSection" href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-drawing-text-typography-h#oh_drawing_typographylayout">OH_Drawing_TypographyLayout</a>接口调用之后调用，否则会返回空指针。不再需要<a
